From your cosy cabin, watch for birds as they flit from tree to tree, or relax in your hot tub as the occasional deer wanders closer. Make a deeper connection to your woodland surroundings with our <a href=\"/things-to-do/forest-ranger-activities\">Forest Rangers</a>, who are brimming over with enthusiasm and are happy to share their knowledge and experiences during unique adventures such as Forest Night Vision.</p></div></div><div class=\"Left\"><div class=\"box\"><div class=\"wrap wrap-carousel\"><div class=\"small-carousel\" id=\"carousel4\">\n<a href=\"#\" class=\"carousel-prev\"><span>prev</span></a><a href=\"#\" class=\"carousel-next\"><span>next</span></a><div class=\"controls\"><div class=\"pages\"></div></div><div class=\"flex-viewport\" style=\"overflow: hidden; background-color: #A4863b;\"></div><div class=\"Left\"><div class=\"bodyText\">How about sleeping in a treehouse? A luxury treehouse, of course. Cross the simple wooden bridge from the main Golden Oak cabin into an exclusive, en-suite room for two. The Golden Oak Treehouse benefits from all the luxuries of our main Golden Oak cabins and sleeps up to 8-10 people. It is currently available at&nbsp;<a href=\"/locations/south-west-england/deerpark-holidays\" shape=\"rect\">Deerpark</a>, <a href=\"/locations/north-of-england/keldy-holidays\" shape=\"rect\">Keldy</a>, <a href=\"/locations/heart-of-england-holidays/sherwood-holidays\" shape=\"rect\">Sherwood Forest</a>,&nbsp;<a href=\"/locations/heart-of-england-holidays/forest-of-dean-holidays\" shape=\"rect\">Forest of Dean</a>,&nbsp;<a href=\"/locations/south-of-england/blackwood-forest-holidays\">Blackwood Forest</a>\nand <a href=\"/locations/south-of-england/thorpe-forest-holidays\">Thorpe Forest</a>.&nbsp;\n<p><br>\n</p></div><div class=\"buttons\"><a
